namespace = colonize_it_e_advanced_region
namespace = colonize_it_e_advanced_region_menu
namespace = colonize_it_e_advanced_region_menu_copy

#譲渡

country_event = {
	id = colonize_it_e_advanced_region.0
	title = colonize_it_e_divite.0.t
	desc = colonize_it_e_divite.0.d
	picture = DEBATE_REPUBLICAN_eventPicture
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = ci_add_region
		country_event = {
			id = colonize_it_e_advanced_region_menu.1
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ci_e_colonies_indexes.t
		country_event = {
			id = ci_e_colonies_indexes.1
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = colonize_it_advanced_region_crear
		every_province = {
			limit = {
				has_province_flag = colonize_it_mark
			}
			clr_province_flag = colonize_it_mark
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = colonize_it_e_advanced_region_menu.1
	title = colonize_it_e_advanced_region.t
	desc = colonize_it_e_advanced_region.desc
	picture = DEBATE_REPUBLICAN_eventPicture
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = ci_filter_trade_company
					has_country_flag = ci_filter_region
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = ci_filter_trade_company
			set_country_flag = ci_filter_region
		}
	}

	option = { #ヨーロッパ
		name = ci_e_colonies_indexes_europa.t
		trigger = {
			any_owned_province = {
				OR = {
					trade_company_region = trade_company_north_sea #北海
					trade_company_region = trade_company_english_channel #イギリス海峡
					trade_company_region = trade_company_bordeaux #ガスコーニュ
					trade_company_region = trade_company_champagne #ブルゴーニュ
					trade_company_region = trade_company_sevilla #イベリア
					trade_company_region = trade_company_valencia #カタルーニャ
					trade_company_region = trade_company_venice #西イタリア
					trade_company_region = trade_company_genua #東イタリア
					trade_company_region = trade_company_rheinland #ラインラント
					trade_company_region = trade_company_wien #オーストリア
					trade_company_region = trade_company_saxony #ザクセン
					trade_company_region = trade_company_lubeck #リューベック
					trade_company_region = trade_company_baltic_sea #バルト
					trade_company_region = trade_company_krakow #ポーランド
					trade_company_region = trade_company_pest #カルパチア
					trade_company_region = trade_company_ragusa #バルカン
					trade_company_region = trade_company_crimea #クリミア
					trade_company_region = trade_company_kiev #キエフ
					trade_company_region = trade_company_novgorod #モスクワ
					trade_company_region = trade_company_white_sea #白海
					trade_company_region = trade_company_kazan #ウラル
					trade_company_region = trade_company_astrakhan #アストラハン
				}
			}
		}
		country_event = {
			id = colonize_it_e_advanced_region_menu.2
		}
    }
	option = { #アフリカ
		name = ci_e_colonies_indexes_africa.t
		trigger = {
			any_owned_province = {
				OR = {
					trade_company_region = trade_company_alexandria #エジプト
					trade_company_region = trade_company_tunis #チュニス
					trade_company_region = trade_company_safi #マグリブ（マグレブ）
					trade_company_region = trade_company_timbuktu #西アフリカ
					trade_company_region = trade_company_west_africa #ギニア
					trade_company_region = trade_company_ethiopia #エチオピア
					trade_company_region = trade_company_east_africa #東アフリカ
					trade_company_region = trade_company_great_lakes #タンザニア
					trade_company_region = trade_company_zambezi #ザンベジ
					trade_company_region = trade_company_kongo #コンゴ
					trade_company_region = trade_company_south_africa #南アフリカ
				}
			}
		}
		country_event = {
			id = colonize_it_e_advanced_region_menu.3
		}
	}
	option = { #アジア
		name = ci_e_colonies_indexes_asia.t
		trigger = {
			any_owned_province = {
				OR = {
					trade_company_region = trade_company_indonesia #インドネシア
					trade_company_region = trade_company_moluccas #モルッカ
					trade_company_region = trade_company_philippines #フィリピン
					trade_company_region = trade_company_indochina #インドシナ
					trade_company_region = trade_company_burma #ビルマ
					trade_company_region = trade_company_constantinople #トルコ
					trade_company_region = trade_company_aleppo #レバント
					trade_company_region = trade_company_basra #マシュリク
					trade_company_region = trade_company_gulf_of_aden #イエメン
					trade_company_region = trade_company_persia #ペルシア
					trade_company_region = trade_company_hormuz #ホルムズ
					trade_company_region = trade_company_lahore #パンジャーブ
					trade_company_region = trade_company_west_india #西インド
					trade_company_region = trade_company_north_india #北インド
					trade_company_region = trade_company_deccan #デカン
					trade_company_region = trade_company_coromandel #コロマンデル
					trade_company_region = trade_company_east_india #東インド
					trade_company_region = trade_company_samarkand #中央アジア
					trade_company_region = trade_company_siberia #シベリア
					trade_company_region = trade_company_yumen #モンゴル
					trade_company_region = trade_company_lhasa #チベット
					trade_company_region = trade_company_north_china #華北
					trade_company_region = trade_company_chengdu #四川
					trade_company_region = trade_company_xian #黄河
					trade_company_region = trade_company_south_china #華南
					trade_company_region = trade_company_east_china #華東
					trade_company_region = trade_company_girin #満州
					trade_company_region = trade_company_nippon #日本
				}
			}
		}
		country_event = {
			id = colonize_it_e_advanced_region_menu.4
		}
	}
	option = { #南北アメリカ
		name = ci_e_colonies_indexes_america.t
		trigger = {
			any_owned_province = {
				OR = {
					colonial_region = colonial_mexico #メキシコ
					colonial_region = colonial_california #カルフォルニア
					colonial_region = colonial_alaska #アラスカ
					colonial_region = colonial_louisiana #ルイジアナ
					colonial_region = colonial_eastern_america #東海岸
					colonial_region = colonial_canada #カナダ
					colonial_region = colonial_the_carribean #カリブ
					colonial_region = colonial_colombia #コロンビア
					colonial_region = colonial_peru #ペルー
					colonial_region = colonial_brazil #ブラジル
					colonial_region = colonial_la_plata #ラプラタ
				}
			}
		}
		country_event = {
			id = colonize_it_e_advanced_region_menu.5
		}
	}
	option = { #オセアニア
		name = ci_e_colonies_indexes_oceania.t
		trigger = {
			any_owned_province = {
				OR = {
					trade_company_region = trade_company_polynesia #太平洋
					colonial_region = colonial_australia #オーストラリア
				}
			}
		}
		country_event = {
			id = colonize_it_e_advanced_region_menu.6
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ci_back
		country_event = {
			id = colonize_it_e_menu.1
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #西欧
	id = colonize_it_e_advanced_region_menu.7
	title = ci_e_colonies_indexes_western_europe.t
	desc = colonize_it_e_advanced_region.desc
	picture = DEBATE_REPUBLICAN_eventPicture
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = ci_e_colonies_indexes.t
		country_event = {
			id = ci_e_colonies_indexes.1
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = colonize_it_advanced_region_crear
		every_province = {
			limit = {
				has_province_flag = colonize_it_mark
			}
			clr_province_flag = colonize_it_mark
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = colonize_it_e_advanced_region_menu_copy.7
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #交易会社地域フィルター1
		name = ci_filter_trade_company_on
		custom_tooltip = ci_filter_trade_company_on.tt
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = ci_filter_trade_company
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = ci_filter_trade_company
			country_event = {
				id = colonize_it_e_advanced_region_menu_copy.7
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #交易会社地域フィルター2
		name = ci_filter_trade_company_off
		custom_tooltip = ci_filter_trade_company_off.tt
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = ci_filter_trade_company
			NOT = { has_country_flag = ci_filter_remove_mark }
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			clr_country_flag = ci_filter_trade_company
			country_event = {
				id = colonize_it_e_advanced_region_menu_copy.7
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #地域フィルター1
		name = ci_filter_region_on
		custom_tooltip = ci_filter_region_on.tt
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = ci_filter_region
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = ci_filter_region
			country_event = {
				id = colonize_it_e_advanced_region_menu_copy.7
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #地域フィルター2
		name = ci_filter_region_off
		custom_tooltip = ci_filter_region_off.tt
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = ci_filter_region
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			clr_country_flag = ci_filter_region
			country_event = {
				id = colonize_it_e_advanced_region_menu_copy.7
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #削除1
		name = ci_filter_remove_region_on
		custom_tooltip = ci_filter_region_on.tt
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = ci_filter_remove_mark
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = ci_filter_remove_mark
			country_event = {
				id = colonize_it_e_advanced_region_menu_copy.7
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #削除2
		name = ci_filter_remove_region_off
		custom_tooltip = ci_filter_region_off.tt
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = ci_filter_remove_mark
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			clr_country_flag = ci_filter_remove_mark
			country_event = {
				id = colonize_it_e_advanced_region_menu_copy.7
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #北海
		name = trade_company_north_sea
		custom_tooltip = colonize_it_e_advanced_region.tt
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = ci_filter_trade_company
			NOT = { has_country_flag = ci_filter_remove_mark }
			any_owned_province = {
				trade_company_region = trade_company_north_sea
			}
		}
		every_owned_province = {
			limit = {
				trade_company_region = trade_company_north_sea
			}
			set_province_flag = colonize_it_mark
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = colonize_it_e_advanced_region_menu_copy.7
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #イギリス海峡
		name = trade_company_english_channel
		custom_tooltip = colonize_it_e_advanced_region.tt
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = ci_filter_trade_company
			NOT = { has_country_flag = ci_filter_remove_mark }
			any_owned_province = {
				trade_company_region = trade_company_english_channel
			}
		}
		every_owned_province = {
			limit = {

		custom_tooltip = colonize_it_e_advanced_region.tt
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = ci_filter_region
			NOT = { has_country_flag = ci_filter_remove_mark }
			any_owned_province = {
				region = british_isles_region
			}
		}
		every_owned_province = {
			limit = {
				region = british_isles_region

		}

				id = colonize_it_e_advanced_region_menu.6
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #地域フィルター1
		name = ci_filter_region_on
		custom_tooltip = ci_filter_region_on.tt
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = ci_filter_region
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = ci_filter_region
			country_event = {
				id = colonize_it_e_advanced_region_menu.6
			}
		}
	}

		name = trade_company_polynesia
		custom_tooltip = colonize_it_e_advanced_region.tt
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = ci_filter_trade_company
			NOT = { has_country_flag = ci_filter_remove_mark }
			any_owned_province = {
				trade_company_region = trade_company_polynesia
			}
		}
		every_owned_province = {
			limit = {
				trade_company_region = trade_company_polynesia
			}
			set_province_flag = colonize_it_mark
		}
		hidden_effect = {
